<div id="review_1703002934" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1703002934" />
    <a title="YA Reads Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1764232-ya-reads-book-reviews"><img alt="YA Reads Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1285429046p2/1764232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1703002934?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="YA Reads Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="YA Reads Book Reviews" href="/user/show/1764232-ya-reads-book-reviews">YA Reads Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1764232-ya-reads-book-reviews?shelf=nichole">nichole</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1703002934" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1662045402680987386">Originally posted on <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.yareads.com'>www.yareads.com</a>, reviewed by Nichole.<br/><br/>The Darkest Lie focuses on Gideon, demon of wrath, an Scarlet, demon of nightmares. We met Scarlet in the previous book in the series. If you've followed this series (which you should be reading them in order,) then you know that Scarlet dropped the bomb on Gideon that they were married. I don't know about you, but that one took me for a bit of a loop. I was definitely caught off guard. It did the trick, though, because I definitely wante</span>
  <span id="freeText1662045402680987386" style="display:none">Originally posted on <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.yareads.com">www.yareads.com</a>, reviewed by Nichole.<br /><br />The Darkest Lie focuses on Gideon, demon of wrath, an Scarlet, demon of nightmares. We met Scarlet in the previous book in the series. If you've followed this series (which you should be reading them in order,) then you know that Scarlet dropped the bomb on Gideon that they were married. I don't know about you, but that one took me for a bit of a loop. I was definitely caught off guard. It did the trick, though, because I definitely wanted to know more about their story!<br /><br /><br />I've been dreading Gideon's story since the very first book in this series, because I had a very bad feeling that I was going to hate decoding every word he said. While I did really enjoy this series, I was correct in that assumption. This book gave me such a headache. Since Gideon is possessed by the demon of Wrath, he can't speak any truths. Honestly, I think the author took that concept way too far. Gideon can't even say someone's real name since his demon considers that a truth and would have to call Scarlet demon instead of angel. That didn't make any sense to me. A like is saying that you want broccoli when you really don't. A lie isn't calling someone by their name or calling someone demon instead of angel, especially when they're not even an angel. I guess that would have made sense if it would have been Gwen, since she really is an Angel. I don't know. I just thought that the author took that whole lying concept a step too far. <br /><br /><br />There were several places in this book that I just wanted to give up and skip to the next book in the series. That's really difficult with this series, though, because there's a constant storyline that continues throughout each book in the series. If you skip one book, you're going to miss a lot. It was really difficult for me, though, because I was constantly having to translate what Gideon was saying. Sometimes, I couldn't figure out what he was saying, and then that author would dedicate a whole paragraph to translate what he said in the true form. I felt like that was a huge waste of space and time. It was just.....ugh. I definitely will never be reading Gideon's book again. <br /><br /><br />On a more positive note, I LOVED how much stuff happened in this book. There was so much going on, so many twists and turns. I was mind blown. I also loved that I would think one thing, and the something else entirely would happen. I'm normally very good about predicting twists and turns, so I was pleasantly surprised!<br /><br /><br />And can I just say Gilliam?! WOAH, BABY! I need more of these two STAT! They better not get one scene per book. I need more of them ASAP!<br /><br /><br />I am getting a bit annoyed that the past couples in this series don't get any face time since their own individual stories. Anya wasn't in this book AT ALL, which was super annoying, and I don't think that Maddox and Ashlyn have had a scene of just the two of them since book 1. Come ON! Seriously? We fall in love with the couples in their own book, and then we still want to see some scenes of them in the future books. <br /><br /><br />Another thing that I was a little disappointed in, and have continued to be in this series, were the sexy scenes. Not all men are the same. They each have their own likes and dislikes, perks and quirks, things that make them unique or nerdy. While we did get to see a little bit about Gideon's differences and preferences in this book, I feel like the sexy scenes are all just kind of blending together. Just doing the deed is not very sexy. Where is the spontaneity or the out of the blue, sexy scene. Or just the cuteness that couples can have every now and then? The author is continuously making these scenes almost exactly the same in every single book. It's quite annoying.<br /><br /><br />Overall, I did really enjoy this book. Mostly, though, that was because of the huge story plot and not because of Gideon and Scarlet. I probably would have enjoyed them as a couple more if I wasn't having to decode every single thing that came out of Gideon's mouth. It was very time tasking! So, I definitely would recommend this book only because it's essential to continue out this amazing paranormal romance series. Be prepared, though, to be very annoyed with every word that comes out of Gid's mouth. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1662045402680987386" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_357448705" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/357448705" />
    <a title="Saly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3192922-saly"><img alt="Saly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1297592167p2/3192922.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/357448705?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Saly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Saly" href="/user/show/3192922-saly">Saly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3192922-saly?shelf=single-titles">single-titles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3192922-saly?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer357448705" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1727277166501664345"><b>SPOILERS</b><br/><b>Rating 3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Ah…such a complicated book and such a twist and good use of the word lie. Gideon is a Lord of the Underworld, his demon Lies, so he cannot speak the truth if he does he experiences pain and 99 % of the time he can tell when people are lying, sadly he can’t tell if Scarlet, the recently captured Titan God who houses the demon nightmare, is lying. She told him she is his wife and then shut down plus they both have the same tattoo. He needs answers so he decides to take her </span>
  <span id="freeText1727277166501664345" style="display:none"><b>SPOILERS</b><br /><b>Rating 3.5 stars</b><br /><br />Ah…such a complicated book and such a twist and good use of the word lie. Gideon is a Lord of the Underworld, his demon Lies, so he cannot speak the truth if he does he experiences pain and 99 % of the time he can tell when people are lying, sadly he can’t tell if Scarlet, the recently captured Titan God who houses the demon nightmare, is lying. She told him she is his wife and then shut down plus they both have the same tattoo. He needs answers so he decides to take her out of the fortress and seduce them out of her. It takes some doing and then in a fit of anger she tells him they had a son named Steel.<br /><br />The story comes out of her slowly, Scarlet was the result of an affair her mother Rhea(wife of Cronus) had with a mortal and grew up in Tartarus, tortured by the other Gods, spending her first few years being a slave to her mother, doing everything for her, even seducing others but her mother and Cronus kept on trying to kill her until a God put up a curse on them, the more they attacked her the older they grew but that didn’t stop them much. He was the guard there and they fell in love and secretly married and he promised to do anything for her (Pandora’s box mission) and then he didn’t return and she was housed with a demon in her, lost for years, her son taken away because of who she was. Once she gained control she again thought of Gideon and his absence made her think he was dead and she grieved for him. She found her son, who had been abused all his life and then saw him being slaughtered by Zeus.<br />When she got free she saw him hale an hearty with other females and her heart broke even further and she tried to be with others but couldn’t.<br /><br />When Gideon learns all of this he is enraged at everything including himself. Scarlet has led a life devoid of any love and he added to it and he hates it that someone messed with his memories and then later comes a twist I was not expecting. Scarlet was the one who had been lied to, there had been no son, no marriage, nothing instead her aunt(memory Goddess) and mother had messed with her, hoping that the life of pain and grief would make her end her life. When she learns all of this she is distraught wanting to leave Gideon but he doesn’t care that she is not his wife or that they were never together, he has come to see her as his. He does want revenge on her aunt and mom though.<br /><br />On other note, Amun and William accompany Aeron on his mission to rescue Legion from hell and Amun is left in a bad condition, his demonic side fully taking over. Strider meanwhile decides to travel to the temple of Unspoken One’s and sees Hunters on the way and captures Haidee, the bait who killed Baden(distrust) and is no longer human, when she escapes he gives the Unspoken One’s the invisibility cloak in return for her. Sienna hates Cronus for putting Wrath into her and is plotting revenge.<br /><br />As usual the book was complicated as hell. There are revelations, Gideon’s demon is female and in love with Nightmare, plus both their demons can leave. I liked the romance, there was plenty of angst and Scarlet tried to put distance between them but Gideon was not having it.<br /><br />I have to say one thing Rhea is despicable, trying to seduce her daughter’s lover and then the memory thing, she deserves to die and I hope to see that.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1727277166501664345" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Smokinhotbooks K.C." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2841223-smokinhotbooks-k-c"><img alt="Smokinhotbooks K.C." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1255740001p2/2841223.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/109041275?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smokinhotbooks K.C." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smokinhotbooks K.C." href="/user/show/2841223-smokinhotbooks-k-c">Smokinhotbooks K.C.</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2841223-smokinhotbooks-k-c?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer109041275" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7239099783461916028"><a href='http://smokinhotbooks.com/blog/2010/07/07/darkestlie-genashowalter/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Read Full Review Here</a> | <a href='http://www.amazon.com/The-Darkest-Lie-ebook/dp/B003SX15KK/ref=tmm_kin_title_0?ie=UTF8&tag=smokinhotbook-20&m=AG56TWVU5XWC2' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kindle</a> | <a href='http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0373774613?ie=UTF8&tag=smokinhotbook-20&linkCode=xm2&camp=1789&creativeASIN=0373774613' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon Print</a><br/><br/><i>Smokinhot Cliff Note: Ok, those of you like me (and K-Khan) and completely forgot the ending in Darkest Passion you are not alone. Darkest Lie starts off with the mysterious Scarlett locked away in the Lords’ dungeon. Gideon can’t quite understand why he is so intrigued by the Keeper of Nightmares, until she mentions she is his wife…</i><br/><br/>Darkest Lie is for the most part told from Gideone’s POV who has to speak in, well, lies. If he tells the truth he is in</span>
  <span id="freeText7239099783461916028" style="display:none"><a href="http://smokinhotbooks.com/blog/2010/07/07/darkestlie-genashowalter/" rel="nofollow noopener">Read Full Review Here</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/The-Darkest-Lie-ebook/dp/B003SX15KK/ref=tmm_kin_title_0?ie=UTF8&amp;tag=smokinhotbook-20&amp;m=AG56TWVU5XWC2" rel="nofollow noopener">Kindle</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0373774613?ie=UTF8&amp;tag=smokinhotbook-20&amp;linkCode=xm2&amp;camp=1789&amp;creativeASIN=0373774613" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon Print</a><br /><br /><i>Smokinhot Cliff Note: Ok, those of you like me (and K-Khan) and completely forgot the ending in Darkest Passion you are not alone. Darkest Lie starts off with the mysterious Scarlett locked away in the Lords’ dungeon. Gideon can’t quite understand why he is so intrigued by the Keeper of Nightmares, until she mentions she is his wife…</i><br /><br />Darkest Lie is for the most part told from Gideone’s POV who has to speak in, well, lies. If he tells the truth he is instantly struck with lots of pain. Now, in the wrong hands this could have read really annoying, but hey, this is Gena Showalter she could write on coupons and I’d still buy ‘em. There is so much going on in Darkest Lie I could probably write a 60 page thesis and barely scratch the surface. Should I create a flow chart? Ok, maybe not. Just making sure ya’ll are awake. Although, I do so like those laser pointers.<br /><br />I’m usually not a fan of old lover’s quarrel plot lines, but it didn’t read like over the top bickering-soap opera . Gideon has no memories of Scarlett (who he calls, Scar, isn’t that cute?), meanwhile Scarlett wants revenge against those who left rotting in a dungeon. Stranded and left to the wolves, she has been waiting for Gideon to return, only to find out that a. he is still alive and b. is a horndog. Not. Cool.<br /><br />Showalter really brings her A-game in what I think is one of her best Lords of the Underworld books. The whole book keeps you on your toes and adds a few interesting twits that had me gasping ‘really?”. I like how she introduces the demons Lies and Nightmares, where see how two immortals and their demons fall in love. (We even get some naughty demon on demon sex…for reals!) Showalter is a master of reintroducing previous characters and not making them appear flat.<br /><br />I believe Darkest Lie is one of Gena Showalter’s best LOTU book, she manages to weave in so many different side plots, while maintaining your interest in the main characters. If you haven’t read this one and have the previous 5 LOTU books on your shelves, shame on you! No, I kid. Seriously, run out and buy it so we can all squee about it on social networks.<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>Mysterious Unveiled</b><br /><br />Why Gideon has blue hair…<br /><br />Cronus is still a dickhead<br /><br />…William….. (that’s all I’m going to say)<br /><br />You have to go here and read Tori’s review quote over at Smexybooks.<br /><br /><br /><b>Unsolved Mysterious</b><br /><br />Will Legion play a part in one of the next Lords book…maybe with Galen?<br /><br />Who thinks Amun should be paired up with one of Harpies sisters? Raises hand<br /><br />Next LOTU book is Darkest Secret (Amun’s story)!!!! And the next one after that is Stryder’s story called Darkest Surrender.<br /><br />Other Reviews<br /><br />That’s What I’m Talking About 3.5/5<br /><br />Smexybooks 5/5<br /><br />Hanging With Bells 3/5</span>

<div id="review_73257926" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/73257926" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2043222-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577660807p2/2043222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/73257926?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/2043222-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer73257926" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9214836816746156770">I can honestly say that as much as I was dying to read this, I wasn't sure how an entire book full of "Gideon Speak" would be to read. It was marvelous. So well-done that I never had an instant where I was unsure of what was said. I loved it and any Lords fans will too! Any Kresley Cole fans will love Carrow's cameo appearance on youtube :)<br/>I think that Gena Showalter is gearing up for something big. Too much was hinted at. (I'm trying to do this review with as few spoilers as possible) I'm super</span>
  <span id="freeText9214836816746156770" style="display:none">I can honestly say that as much as I was dying to read this, I wasn't sure how an entire book full of "Gideon Speak" would be to read. It was marvelous. So well-done that I never had an instant where I was unsure of what was said. I loved it and any Lords fans will too! Any Kresley Cole fans will love Carrow's cameo appearance on youtube :)<br />I think that Gena Showalter is gearing up for something big. Too much was hinted at. (I'm trying to do this review with as few spoilers as possible) I'm super curious how Siena will escape Cronus, and if she will go stay with Paris. Curious how Amun will survive what happened to him, and to see if Lysander will be forced to hunt him down...and by the way Lysander is one hero who I LOVE in his book "The Darkest Angel," but man in the past 2? I just want to kick him in the shin!<br />Anyone familiar with this series will recognize Scarlet from the Darkest Passion. She says that she is Gideon's wife...or was? We aren't really given too much to go on. One thing that's too funny is she takes a lot of what he says literally even though she knows he has to lie. A few times, though, Gideon's demon Lies actually tells the truth in his head, and even that causes untold pain.<br />I think that Gideon and Scarlet had a great give-and-take relationship. Sometimes I find when the hero/heroine go back and forth too often, I get annoyed with each of them. In Gena Showalter's wonderful way, she had me sympathizing with them, enjoying the passion, the anger, the betrayal. I just loved it. In fact, when we find out the "Big Lie" as I'll call it, turns out poor Scarlet, daughter of Rhea, was just a big giant pawn in her aunt, mother, and Cronus' boredom. They used her to break up the monotony of their eternal Titanic lives. When I found out all that had been done to her, I just wanted to cry for her. <br />And Gideon! Wow, when the "Big Lie" is revealed by (of all people, er gods, Cronus) you not only want to weep for Scarlet, but for Gideon and all Scarlet had accused him of. She and he had a great chemistry and the sexual tension was steamy even without sex until almost the end. There were plenty of encounters where the steam factor cranked up. <br />A wonderful read, another fantastic Lords book by Gena Showalter, and wow, gotta love Gideon.<br />look for my full review at the demonlover website:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.demonloversbooksandmore.com/2010/07/book-review-darkest-lie-by-gena.html">http://www.demonloversbooksandmore.co...</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9214836816746156770" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PhESFq+AVW6mJ9u47cvoEA2wLJvF70xZB11V+9S+k2VulXLorDTYjiqI7Q6obCOpTtRcDpnVsft3fSFK9TeNjg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('S5ecUWwTa3kyAvtTIuBEaxEWTjgH5kEzzvmiODQtNxIbE/yvb6fmmb6tzeVnR4/SUnI+rVvcvJG+2daJFaQp+Q==')})
  }

But once he secures the key to his redemption, the halfling Holly Ashwin, Cade finds that the woman he thought he could use for his own ends and then forget haunts him as much as his past.\n\nA tormented warrior she should fear, but can\'t deny... \nRaised as a human, Holly never knew that some frightening legends are real until she encounters a brutal demon who inexplicably guards her like a treasure.
